[30;1m35 | [0m[35mdef _clip_by_l2_norm(x: Array, max_norm: float) -> Array:[0m
[30;1m36 | [0m[35m  """Clip gradients to maximum l2 norm `max_norm`."""[0m
[30;1m37 | [0m[35m  # Compute the sum of squares and find out where things are zero.[0m
[30;1m38 | [0m[35m  sum_sq = jnp.sum(jnp.vdot(x, x))[0m
[30;1m39 | [0m[35m  nonzero = sum_sq > 0[0m
[30;1m40 | [0m[35m[0m
